## assistant (2026-02-02T13:32:04.181Z)

Here’s a **weekly business review (based on the #🇧🇷-davi Discord channel)** for **last week (Mon Jan 26 → Sun Feb 1)**. I’m focusing on *what happened, decisions made, and what’s still open*.

---

## Executive summary (week in one page)
- The week was dominated by **ops + fulfillment cleanup**: fixing/validating **FB Lead Form → GoHighLevel** flow, running a **full client sweep**, and pushing multiple clients toward “ads live + stable leads.”
- You and Davi also progressed **cold SMS / lead sourcing ops**, and started building **proof + website leverage** (past client results → social proof).
- End of week included **payroll logistics** for Davi (Wise, prorated Jan pay) and **Braymiller/Susquehanna launch blockers**.

---

## What actually happened (chronological highlights)

### Mon (Jan 26) — Lead delivery fire + onboarding issues
- **FB/GHL integration problems** were front-and-center.
  - Davi was **manually importing missing leads** into GoHighLevel and asked if he should **push them into pipeline/workflows** so automations follow up (you confirmed they should be added as if they filled the form; “drip mode” suggested: spacing leads so owners don’t get flooded).
  - Davi flagged the issue as deeper (credentials/permission-related, possibly tied to account restrictions) and said it may require **client-side permissions** to resolve.
- **Eco Concrete onboarding**: you flagged it as an “L” / delayed onboarding, client unhappy; Davi asked for Loom/live help to create the GHL location + get campaigns live.
- You reviewed Eco Concrete ads and felt creatives were **too vague/weak**; suggested simpler direct-response style might outperform.

### Tue (Jan 27) — Stabilization + sweep completion + cold SMS doc
- Davi pushed urgency: **ads must be live** for key clients (Ashton, BE Decking, Concept II, STP, Susq) while lead delivery is sorted (manual import if needed).
- You personally **tested lead forms via Facebook Lead Ads testing tool** and reported all key clients looked OK (Concept II, Ashton, STP, Susq, BE Decking).
- Davi had prolonged back-and-forth with **Facebook support vs GHL support** (“each blames the other”), spent hours, and paused the FB support thread with a window to keep testing.
- Davi completed a **full sweep of active clients** (you later praised him for catching up and expected smoother operations going forward).
- Cold SMS / sales ops:
  - A **Notion doc: “January 27 Cold SMS Optimization”** was created/shared.
  - There was discussion about **lead quality + duplicates**; you noted only ~24% duplicates (good), and clarified duplicates are acceptable in tracking because follow-ups/reschedules can create duplicates.

### Wed (Jan 28) — Systems tightening (forms/tracking) + Cornerstone message drafting
- Operational cleanup continued:
  - Davi reported **Shiva access removal** (some limits: Discord permissions, Business Portfolio needed your confirmation).
  - You gave Davi a structured instruction set: **pause Redwood and do a thorough sweep** across all active clients; only flag what needs action.
- **Sales tracking sheet hygiene**:
  - You gave rules: only confirmed sales calls, no interviews, outcome must be filled if call “showed,” etc.
  - Davi mislogged/over-logged initially; you corrected process and recorded a Loom walkthrough.
  - You later asked to **remove “no duplicates” rule** because duplicates can be legitimate.
- **STP lead form updates**:
  - Davi updated the form and confirmed Terms/Privacy pages OK.
  - Discussion about disqualifying “landlord” leads via conditional logic.
  - You provided a Notion SOP link (“How to Update Lead Form”) and emphasized re-mapping fields after publish.
- **Cornerstone Restorations retention/offboarding messaging**:
  - Lots of iteration on wording: you pushed for focusing on **leads + downstream results**, not impressions/reach.
  - Goal: ask them how many leads → appointments → closes; note you lacked feedback needed to optimize; remind contract end date is Jan 29.
